First the grocery store brands- Pantene Pro-V, Herbal Essences (can you say horrible RASH?), John Frieda Frizz Ease. Nothing worked to get my hair sleek and smooth. Then came cheaper salon brands: Bed-Head, Catwalk, Regis, Joico. Then came the really pricey stuff: K-Pak, Wen, Biolage. All were 'okay' and helped my hair to look healthier, but still not smooth and controlled. I gave up, I was a chronic victim of Ponytail headaches, trapped in a world left without style and unable to partake in fun, new hairstyles. I bought a great flat iron, a step above Chi, even. That helped some but killed the one thing my hair had going for it- healthy looking and soft. Two kids and a broken thyroid later and it was now limp, thinning and dull as well.<br /><br />Enter in It's a 10. A friend of mine who is a stylist gave me the deep treatment conditioner and shampoo, as well as the Miracle leave in. It changed my hair. I no longer have to choose between crunchy, heavily gelled curls or broken, frizzy straightened hair. I can do either and my hair, with regular trims look gorgeous and smells even MORE gorgeous either way. Nothing can repair broken hair, hair is dead but this product keeps freshly trimmed locks healthy and prevents breakage and split ends unlike any other. I've even used Wen because I have such dry hair but even that pales in comparison.<br /><br />My regimen includes the following; Wash with Keratin shampoo, condition with Daily Keratin conditioner. I suggest the Keratin for people who colour or straighten their hair because it will improve elasticity and prevent styling breakage. Otherwise, the normal daily products work great. I then mist with the Keratin Miracle leave in. I do this every OTHER day. Before I style, on damp or dry hair I add THREE drops of the Miracle Argon Oil to my long, mid back length hair and work in well. If I am going curly I add it to wet hair, scrunch, two more sprays leave in and up in a towel. Soft, smooth curls will await you. If there's some frizz a little more of each the oil and spray will tame that. On straight days I do the same routine, letting my hair towel dry as long as possible before blow drying with my fingers (again, less breakage and frizzing) and then flat iron adding extra oil as I go.<br /><br />You do NOT NEED TO SHAMPOO EVERY DAY. People with 'oily' hair have oily hair because they're over washing. It will take two weeks of letting it go three days or more without using shampoo but your scalp will adjust and stop over producing oil trying to overcompensate for over washing. Shampoo every 2-3 days and on non shampoo days simply \\"wash\\" your hair with the Daily conditioner. Work it through your hair thoroughly, rubbing the scalp. Rinse well for five minutes in COOL water. A little leave in at the length, not the scalp and your hair will thank you. Trust me, this WILL work after a few attempts. I know it feels weird and gross the first few times but that's your scalp adjusting to not needing to make so much extra oil. The daily conditioner is gentle and light enough to be the perfect cleansing conditioner, just like Wen but BETTER! Deep condition once a week with one of your shampoo days and in a month you will have all new hair.<br /><br />If it can save mine, it WILL save yours! My thin spots are even growing new hair again because, well...my thyroid is now under control, but also because my scalp and it's PH and hair follicles are all healthier. It's worth the cost and easy to afford on Amazon, plus you need so little of everything.
